	fire_only_once = yes

		name = BAS.1.a
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

				mountaineers = { x = 1 y = 2 }

country_event = { 
	id = BAS.18
	title = BAS.18.t 
	desc = BAS.18.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_BAS_gernika
	trigger = {
		tag = BAS
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1936.11.4
				date < 1936.12.4
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1937.27.3
				date < 1937.28.3
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1938.16.4
				date < 1938.17.4
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1939.8.4
				date < 1939.9.4
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1940.23.3
				date < 1940.24.3
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1941.12.4
				date < 1941.13.4
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1942.4.4
				date < 1942.5.4
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = BAS.18.a
		add_political_power = 15
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = BAS.1800
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
}
